<div class="postcell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
                    
<p>In my Node application I need to remove a directory which has some files, but <a href="https://nodejs.org/api/fs.html#fs_fs_rmdir_path_callback"><code>fs.rmdir</code></a> only works on empty directories. How can I do this?</p>
    </div>

                        <li id="comment-97759510" class="comment js-comment " data-comment-id="97759510">
        <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

                    <span title="number of &#x27;useful comment&#x27; votes received"
                            class="cool">2</span>

        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">In short: <code>fs.readdir(dirPath)</code> for an array of paths in a folder, iterate through <code>fs.unlink(filename)</code> to delete each file, and then finally <code>fs.rmdir(dirPath)</code> to delete the now-empty folder. If you need to recurse, check <code>fs.lstat(filename).isDirectory()</code>.</span>
                
&ndash;&nbsp;<a href="/users/1129420/iono"
                       title="2,352 reputation"
                       class="comment-user">iono</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><span title="2019-04-05 03:38:26Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0" class="relativetime-clean">Apr 5 '19 at 3:38</span></span>
            </div>
        </div>

<a name="18052969"></a>
<div id="answer-18052969" class="answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="18052969"  itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="18052969">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="328">328</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/18052969/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>There is a module for this called <code>rimraf</code> (<a href="https://npmjs.org/package/rimraf" rel="noreferrer">https://npmjs.org/package/rimraf</a>). It provides the same functionality as <code>rm -Rf</code></p>

<p><strong>Async</strong> usage:</p>

<pre><code>var rimraf = require("rimraf");
rimraf("/some/directory", function () { console.log("done"); });
</code></pre>

<p><strong>Sync</strong> usage:</p>

<pre><code>rimraf.sync("/some/directory");
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2013-08-05T07:43:23"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p><strong>To remove folder synchronously</strong></p>

<pre><code>const fs = require('fs');
const Path = require('path');

const deleteFolderRecursive = function(path) {
  if (fs.existsSync(path)) {
    fs.readdirSync(path).forEach((file, index) =&gt; {
      const curPath = Path.join(path, file);
      if (fs.lstatSync(curPath).isDirectory()) { // recurse
        deleteFolderRecursive(curPath);
      } else { // delete file
        fs.unlinkSync(curPath);
      }
    });
    fs.rmdirSync(path);
  }
};
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<h1>As of 2019...</h1>

<p>As of <a href="https://nodejs.org/en/blog/release/v12.10.0/" rel="noreferrer">Node.js <strong>12.10.0</strong></a>, <a href="https://nodejs.org/api/fs.html#fs_fs_rmdir_path_options" rel="noreferrer"><code>fs.rmdirSync</code></a> supports a <code>recursive</code> options, so you can finally do:</p>

<pre class="lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>fs.rmdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
</code></pre>

<p>Where the <code>recursive</code> option deletes the entire directory recursively.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2019-09-10T07:41:26"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<div id="answer-36934291" class="answer" data-answerid="36934291"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="36934291">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="171">171</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/36934291/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Most of the people using <code>fs</code> with Node.js would like functions close to the "Unix way" of dealing with files. I'm using <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra" rel="noreferrer">fs-extra</a> to bring all the cool stuff :</p>

<blockquote>
  <p>fs-extra contains methods that aren't included in the vanilla Node.js
  fs package. Such as mkdir -p, cp -r, and rm -rf.</p>
</blockquote>

<p>Even better, <strong>fs-extra</strong> is a drop in replacement for native fs. All methods in fs are unmodified and attached to it.
It means that you can replace fs by <strong>fs-extra</strong> :</p>

<pre><code>// this can be replaced
const fs = require('fs')

// by this
const fs = require('fs-extra')
</code></pre>

<p>And then you can remove a folder this way:</p>

<pre><code>fs.removeSync('/tmp/myFolder'); 
//or
fs.remove('/tmp/myFolder', callback);
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2016-04-29T09:13:29"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">

                <span class="comment-copy">for the sync version you need <code>removeSync(&#39;&#47;tmp&#47;myFolder&#39;)</code></span>
                
&ndash;&nbsp;<a href="/users/5330805/olidem"
                       title="1,000 reputation"
                       class="comment-user">olidem</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><span title="2020-05-22 16:18:53Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0" class="relativetime-clean">May 22 at 16:18</span></span>
                        <span title="this comment was edited 2 times">
                            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 14 14"><path d="M11.1 1.71l1.13 1.12c.2.2.2.51 0 .71L11.1 4.7 9.21 2.86l1.17-1.15c.2-.2.51-.2.71 0zM2 10.12l6.37-6.43 1.88 1.88L3.88 12H2v-1.88z"/></svg>

<div id="answer-42505874" class="answer" data-answerid="42505874"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>My modified answer from @oconnecp (<a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/25069828/3027390">https://stackoverflow.com/a/25069828/3027390</a>)</p>

<p>Uses path.join for better cross-platform experience.
So, don't forget to require it.</p>

<pre><code>var path = require('path');
</code></pre>

<p>Also renamed function to <code>rimraf</code> ;)</p>

<pre><code>/**
 * Remove directory recursively
 * @param {string} dir_path
 * @see https://stackoverflow.com/a/42505874/3027390
 */
function rimraf(dir_path) {
    if (fs.existsSync(dir_path)) {
        fs.readdirSync(dir_path).forEach(function(entry) {
            var entry_path = path.join(dir_path, entry);
            if (fs.lstatSync(entry_path).isDirectory()) {
                rimraf(entry_path);
            } else {
                fs.unlinkSync(entry_path);
            }
        });
        fs.rmdirSync(dir_path);
    }
}
</code></pre>
    </div>

<a name="55661804"></a>
<div id="answer-55661804" class="answer" data-answerid="55661804"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="55661804">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="17">17</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/55661804/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>I don't usually resurrect old threads but there is a <em>lot</em> on churn here and sans the rimraf answer these all seem overly complicated to me.</p>

<p>First in modern Node (>= v8.0.0) you can simplify the process using only node core modules, fully asynchronous, and parallelize the unlinking of files concurrently all in a function of five lines and still keep readability:</p>

<pre><code>const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { promisify } = require('util');
const readdir = promisify(fs.readdir);
const rmdir = promisify(fs.rmdir);
const unlink = promisify(fs.unlink);

exports.rmdirs = async function rmdirs(dir) {
  let entries = await readdir(dir, { withFileTypes: true });
  await Promise.all(entries.map(entry =&gt; {
    let fullPath = path.join(dir, entry.name);
    return entry.isDirectory() ? rmdirs(fullPath) : unlink(fullPath);
  }));
  await rmdir(dir);
};
</code></pre>

<p>On another note a guard for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Directory_traversal_attack" rel="noreferrer">path traversal attacks</a> is inappropriate for this function because</p>

<ol>
<li>It is out of scope based on the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Single_responsibility_principle" rel="noreferrer">Single Responsibility Principle</a>.</li>
<li>Should be handled by the caller <em>not</em> this function. This is akin to the command-line <code>rm -rf</code> in that it takes an argument and will allow the user to <code>rm -rf /</code> if asked to. It would be the responsibility of a script to guard not the <code>rm</code> program itself.</li>
<li>This function would be unable to determine such an attack since it does not have a frame of reference. Again that is the responsibility of the caller who would have the context of intent which would provide it a reference to compare the path traversal.</li>
<li>Sym-links are not a concern as <code>.isDirectory()</code> is <code>false</code> for sym-links and are unlinked not recursed into.</li>
</ol>

<p>Last but not least, there is a rare race condition that the recursion could error if one of the entries was unlinked or deleted <em>outside</em> this script at just the right time while this recursion is running. Since this scenario is not typical in most environments it can likely be overlooked. However, if required (for some edge cases) this issue can be mitigated with this slightly more complex example:</p>

<pre><code>exports.rmdirs = async function rmdirs(dir) {
  let entries = await readdir(dir, { withFileTypes: true });
  let results = await Promise.all(entries.map(entry =&gt; {
    let fullPath = path.join(dir, entry.name);
    let task = entry.isDirectory() ? rmdirs(fullPath) : unlink(fullPath);
    return task.catch(error =&gt; ({ error }));
  }));
  results.forEach(result =&gt; {
    // Ignore missing files/directories; bail on other errors
    if (result &amp;&amp; result.error.code !== 'ENOENT') throw result.error;
  });
  await rmdir(dir);
};
</code></pre>

<p><strong>EDIT:</strong> Make <code>isDirectory()</code> a function. Remove the actual directory at the end. Fix missing recursion.</p>
    </div>

    <li id="comment-100481652" class="comment js-comment " data-comment-id="100481652">
        <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">@GTPV Why? This increases the responsibility of this function. <code>readdir</code> will throw an error as it should. If you <code>rmdir non-existing-dir</code> the exit code is an error. It would be the responsibility of the consumer to try/catch. This is the same method described in the Node docs when it comes to using fs functions. They expect you to try/catch and look at the error&#39;s <code>code</code> to determine what to do. An extra check introduces a race condition.</span>
                
&ndash;&nbsp;<a href="/users/227176/sukima"
                       title="9,377 reputation"
                       class="comment-user">Sukima</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><span title="2019-07-10 14:15:57Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0" class="relativetime-clean">Jul 10 '19 at 14:15</span></span>
            </div>
        </div>
    </li>
    <li id="comment-100482960" class="comment js-comment " data-comment-id="100482960">
        <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
            <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">I definitely see your point. I would expect though intuitively that attempting to delete a folder which does not exists would be successful as it would simply do nothing. No race condition if the synchronous version of <code>fs.exists</code> is used. P.S. this is a great solution.</span>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Here is an async version of <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/32197381/806777">@SharpCoder's answer</a></p>

<pre><code>const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

function deleteFile(dir, file) {
    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
        var filePath = path.join(dir, file);
        fs.lstat(filePath, function (err, stats) {
            if (err) {
                return reject(err);
            }
            if (stats.isDirectory()) {
                resolve(deleteDirectory(filePath));
            } else {
                fs.unlink(filePath, function (err) {
                    if (err) {
                        return reject(err);
                    }
                    resolve();
                });
            }
        });
    });
};

function deleteDirectory(dir) {
    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
        fs.access(dir, function (err) {
            if (err) {
                return reject(err);
            }
            fs.readdir(dir, function (err, files) {
                if (err) {
                    return reject(err);
                }
                Promise.all(files.map(function (file) {
                    return deleteFile(dir, file);
                })).then(function () {
                    fs.rmdir(dir, function (err) {
                        if (err) {
                            return reject(err);
                        }
                        resolve();
                    });
                }).catch(reject);
            });
        });
    });
};
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div id="answer-25069828" class="answer" data-answerid="25069828"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="25069828">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/25069828/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>I wrote this function called remove folder.  It will recursively remove all the files and folders in a location.  The only package it requires is async.</p>

<pre><code>var async = require('async');

function removeFolder(location, next) {
    fs.readdir(location, function (err, files) {
        async.each(files, function (file, cb) {
            file = location + '/' + file
            fs.stat(file, function (err, stat) {
                if (err) {
                    return cb(err);
                }
                if (stat.isDirectory()) {
                    removeFolder(file, cb);
                } else {
                    fs.unlink(file, function (err) {
                        if (err) {
                            return cb(err);
                        }
                        return cb();
                    })
                }
            })
        }, function (err) {
            if (err) return next(err)
            fs.rmdir(location, function (err) {
                return next(err)
            })
        })
    })
}
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/49006652/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>If you are using node 8+ want asyncronicity and don't want external dependencies, here is the async/await version:</p>

<pre><code>const path = require('path');
const fs = require('fs');
const util = require('util');

const readdir = util.promisify(fs.readdir);
const lstat = util.promisify(fs.lstat);
const unlink = util.promisify(fs.unlink);
const rmdir = util.promisify(fs.rmdir);

const removeDir = async (dir) =&gt; {
    try {
        const files = await readdir(dir);
        await Promise.all(files.map(async (file) =&gt; {
            try {
                const p = path.join(dir, file);
                const stat = await lstat(p);
                if (stat.isDirectory()) {
                    await removeDir(p);
                } else {
                    await unlink(p);
                    console.log(`Removed file ${p}`);
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error(err);
            }
        }))
        await rmdir(dir);
        console.log(`Removed dir ${dir}`);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
    }
}
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2018-02-27T10:39:09"></time>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Async version of <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/32197381/6304917">@SharpCoder's answer</a> using fs.promises:</p>

<pre><code>const fs = require('fs');
const afs = fs.promises;

const deleteFolderRecursive = async path =&gt;  {
    if (fs.existsSync(path)) {
        for (let entry of await afs.readdir(path)) {
            const curPath = path + "/" + entry;
            if ((await afs.lstat(curPath)).isDirectory())
                await deleteFolderRecursive(curPath);
            else await afs.unlink(curPath);
        }
        await afs.rmdir(path);
    }
};
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div id="answer-35698254" class="answer" data-answerid="35698254"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="35698254">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>I reached here while trying to get over with the <code>gulp</code> and I'm writing for further reaches.</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/gulp-clean" rel="nofollow"><code>gulp-clean</code></a> deprecated for <code>gulp-rimraf</code></li>
<li><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/gulp-rimraf" rel="nofollow"><code>gulp-rimraf</code></a> deprecated in favor of <a href="https://github.com/gulpjs/gulp/blob/master/docs/recipes/delete-files-folder.md" rel="nofollow"><code>delete-files-folders</code></a></li>
</ul>

<p>When you want to delete files and folders using <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/del" rel="nofollow"><code>del</code></a>, you should append <code>/**</code> for recursive deletion.</p>

<pre><code>gulp.task('clean', function () {
    return del(['some/path/to/delete/**']);
});
</code></pre>
    </div>

<a name="47927004"></a>
<div id="answer-47927004" class="answer" data-answerid="47927004"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="47927004">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="2">2</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/47927004/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>The de facto package is <code>rimraf</code>, but here is my tiny async version:</p>

<pre><code>const fs = require('fs')
const path = require('path')
const Q = require('q')

function rmdir (dir) {
  return Q.nfcall(fs.access, dir, fs.constants.W_OK)
    .then(() =&gt; {
      return Q.nfcall(fs.readdir, dir)
        .then(files =&gt; files.reduce((pre, f) =&gt; pre.then(() =&gt; {
          var sub = path.join(dir, f)
          return Q.nfcall(fs.lstat, sub).then(stat =&gt; {
            if (stat.isDirectory()) return rmdir(sub)
            return Q.nfcall(fs.unlink, sub)
          })
        }), Q()))
    })
    .then(() =&gt; Q.nfcall(fs.rmdir, dir))
}

</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<a name="57834155"></a>
<div id="answer-57834155" class="answer" data-answerid="57834155"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="57834155">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="2">2</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/57834155/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>In the latest version of Node.js (12.10.0 or later), the <code>rmdir</code> style functions <a href="https://nodejs.org/api/fs.html#fs_fs_rmdir_path_options_callback" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><code>fs.rmdir()</code></a>, <a href="https://nodejs.org/api/fs.html#fs_fs_rmdirsync_path_options" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><code>fs.rmdirSync()</code></a>, and <a href="https://nodejs.org/api/fs.html#fs_fspromises_rmdir_path_options" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><code>fs.promises.rmdir()</code></a> have a new experimental option <code>recursive</code> that allows deleting non-empty directories, e.g.</p>

<pre class="lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>fs.rmdir(path, { recursive: true });
</code></pre>

<p>The related PR on GitHub: <a href="https://github.com/nodejs/node/pull/29168" rel="nofollow noreferrer">https://github.com/nodejs/node/pull/29168</a></p>
    </div>

<div id="answer-60161321" class="answer" data-answerid="60161321"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="60161321">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/60161321/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>According to the <a href="https://nodejs.org/api/fs.html#fs_fspromises_rmdir_path_options" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><code>fs</code> documentation</a>, <code>fsPromises</code> currently provides the <code>recursive</code> option on an experimental basis, which, at least in my own case on Windows, removes the directory and any files therein.</p>

<pre><code>fsPromises.rmdir(path, {
  recursive: true
})
</code></pre>

<p>Does <code>recursive: true</code> remove the files on Linux and MacOS?</p>
    </div>

<div id="answer-57340504" class="answer" data-answerid="57340504"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="57340504">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="1">1</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/57340504/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p><strong>Ultra-speed and fail-proof</strong></p>

<p>You can use the <code>lignator</code> package (<a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/lignator" rel="nofollow noreferrer">https://www.npmjs.com/package/lignator</a>), it's faster than any async code (e.g. rimraf) and more fail-proof (especially in Windows, where file removal is not instantaneous and files might be locked by other processes).</p>

<blockquote>
  <p><em>4,36 GB of data, 28 042 files, 4 217 folders on Windows removed in <strong>15 seconds vs rimraf's 60 seconds</strong> on old HDD.</em></p>
</blockquote>

<pre><code>const lignator = require('lignator');

lignator.remove('./build/');
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2019-08-03T17:09:48"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<div id="answer-57388385" class="answer" data-answerid="57388385"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">

        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="57388385">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p><strong>Sync folder remove with the files or only a file.</strong><br><br>
I am not much of a giver nor a contributor but I couldn't find a good solution of this problem and I had to find my way... so I hope you'll like it :) <br><br>
Works perfect for me with any number of nested directories and sub directories. Caution for the scope of 'this' when recursing the function, your implementation may be different. In my case this function stays into the return of another function that's why I am calling it with this.
<br><br></p>

<pre><code>    const fs = require('fs');

    deleteFileOrDir(path, pathTemp = false){
            if (fs.existsSync(path)) {
                if (fs.lstatSync(path).isDirectory()) {
                    var files = fs.readdirSync(path);
                    if (!files.length) return fs.rmdirSync(path);
                    for (var file in files) {
                        var currentPath = path + "/" + files[file];
                        if (!fs.existsSync(currentPath)) continue;
                        if (fs.lstatSync(currentPath).isFile()) {
                            fs.unlinkSync(currentPath);
                            continue;
                        }
                        if (fs.lstatSync(currentPath).isDirectory() &amp;&amp; !fs.readdirSync(currentPath).length) {
                            fs.rmdirSync(currentPath);
                        } else {
                            this.deleteFileOrDir(currentPath, path);
                        }
                    }
                    this.deleteFileOrDir(path);
                } else {
                    fs.unlinkSync(path);
                }
            }
            if (pathTemp) this.deleteFileOrDir(pathTemp);
        }
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>2020 Update</p>

<p>From version 12.10.0 <em>recursiveOption</em> has been added for options.</p>

<p>Note that <strong>recursive deletion is experimental</strong>.</p>

<p>So you would do for sync:</p>

<pre><code>fs.rmdirSync(dir, {recursive: true});
</code></pre>

<p>or for async:</p>

<pre><code>fs.rmdir(dir, {recursive: true});
</code></pre>
    </div>

    <div class="post-layout">

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Just use <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/rmdir" rel="nofollow">rmdir module</a>! it's easy and simple.</p>

<div id="answer-43120504" class="answer" data-answerid="43120504"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="43120504">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/43120504/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Another alternative is using the <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-promise" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><code>fs-promise</code></a> module that provides promisified versions of the <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><code>fs-extra</code></a> modules</p>

<p>you could then write like this example:</p>

<pre><code>const { remove, mkdirp, writeFile, readFile } = require('fs-promise')
const { join, dirname } = require('path')

async function createAndRemove() {
  const content = 'Hello World!'
  const root = join(__dirname, 'foo')
  const file = join(root, 'bar', 'baz', 'hello.txt')

  await mkdirp(dirname(file))
  await writeFile(file, content)
  console.log(await readFile(file, 'utf-8'))
  await remove(join(__dirname, 'foo'))
}

createAndRemove().catch(console.error)
</code></pre>

<p>note: async/await requires a recent nodejs version (7.6+)</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<a name="48981031"></a>
<div id="answer-48981031" class="answer" data-answerid="48981031"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="48981031">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>
        <div class="js-vote-count grid--cell fc-black-500 fs-title grid fd-column ai-center" itemprop="upvoteCount" data-value="0">0</div>
        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/48981031/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>A quick and dirty way <strong>(maybe for testing)</strong> could be to directly use the <code>exec</code> or <code>spawn</code> method to invoke OS call to remove the directory. Read more on <a href="https://nodejs.org/api/child_process.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">NodeJs child_process</a>.</p>

<pre><code>let exec = require('child_process').exec
exec('rm -Rf /tmp/*.zip', callback)
</code></pre>

<p><strong>Downsides are:</strong></p>

<ol>
<li>You are depending on underlying OS i.e. the same method would run in unix/linux but probably not in windows.</li>
<li>You cannot hijack the process on conditions or errors. You just give the task to underlying OS and wait for the exit code to be returned.</li>
</ol>

<p><strong>Benefits:</strong></p>

<ol>
<li>These processes can run asynchronously.</li>
<li>You can listen for the output/error of the command, hence command output is not lost. If operation is not completed, you can check the error code and retry.</li>
</ol>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2018-02-26T03:29:32"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">Perfect for when you write script and don&#39;t want to install dependencies because you&#39;re about to delete this script in 30 seconds after you deleted all your files!!</span>
                
&ndash;&nbsp;<a href="/users/530709/mathias"
                       title="1,454 reputation"
                       class="comment-user">Mathias</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><span title="2018-11-01 20:18:23Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0" class="relativetime-clean">Nov 1 '18 at 20:18</span></span>
            </div>
        </div>
    </li>
    <li id="comment-98608505" class="comment js-comment " data-comment-id="98608505">
        <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
            <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">There are always ways to mess up and delete the root filesystem. In this case OP can remove the <code>-f</code> flag to be safe, or make sure while typing that he/she is not going to delete everything. <code>exec + rm</code> is a valid and useful command in node which I use often during testing.</span>
                
&ndash;&nbsp;<a href="/users/1834562/rash"
                       title="5,549 reputation"
                       class="comment-user">Rash</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><span title="2019-05-04 03:49:26Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0" class="relativetime-clean">May 4 '19 at 3:49</span></span>

<div id="answer-39316980" class="answer" data-answerid="39316980"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="39316980">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>I wish there was a way to do this without additional modules for something so minuscule and common, but this is the best I could come up with.</p>

<p>Update:
Should now work on Windows (tested Windows 10), and should also work on Linux/Unix/BSD/Mac systems.</p>

<pre><code>const
    execSync = require("child_process").execSync,
    fs = require("fs"),
    os = require("os");

let removeDirCmd, theDir;

removeDirCmd = os.platform() === 'win32' ? "rmdir /s /q " : "rm -rf ";

theDir = __dirname + "/../web-ui/css/";

// WARNING: Do not specify a single file as the windows rmdir command will error.
if (fs.existsSync(theDir)) {
    console.log(' removing the ' + theDir + ' directory.');
    execSync(removeDirCmd + '"' + theDir + '"', function (err) {
        console.log(err);
    });
}
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2016-09-04T12:35:41"></time>

<a name="52931558"></a>
<div id="answer-52931558" class="answer" data-answerid="52931558"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="52931558">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

        <button class="js-vote-down-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is not useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Down vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 10h32L18 26 2 10z"/></svg></button>

    
            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/52931558/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>This is one approach using promisify and two help functions (to and toAll) to resolve the promise.</p>

<p>It does all actions asynchrounous.</p>

<pre class="lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>const fs = require('fs');
const { promisify } = require('util');
const to = require('./to');
const toAll = require('./toAll');

const readDirAsync = promisify(fs.readdir);
const rmDirAsync = promisify(fs.rmdir);
const unlinkAsync = promisify(fs.unlink);

/**
    * @author Aécio Levy
    * @function removeDirWithFiles
    * @usage: remove dir with files
    * @param {String} path
    */
const removeDirWithFiles = async path =&gt; {
    try {
        const file = readDirAsync(path);
        const [error, files] = await to(file);
        if (error) {
            throw new Error(error)
        }
        const arrayUnlink = files.map((fileName) =&gt; {
            return unlinkAsync(`${path}/${fileName}`);
        });
        const [errorUnlink, filesUnlink] = await toAll(arrayUnlink);
        if (errorUnlink) {
            throw new Error(errorUnlink);
        }
        const deleteDir = rmDirAsync(path);
        const [errorDelete, result] = await to(deleteDir);
        if (errorDelete) {
            throw new Error(errorDelete);
        }
    } catch (err) {
        console.log(err)
    }
}; 
</code></pre>

    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/57567009/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>//without use of any third party lib </p>

<pre><code>const fs = require('fs');
var FOLDER_PATH = "./dirname";
var files = fs.readdirSync(FOLDER_PATH);
files.forEach(element =&gt; {
    fs.unlinkSync(FOLDER_PATH + "/" + element);
});
fs.rmdirSync(FOLDER_PATH);
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div id="answer-58454734" class="answer" data-answerid="58454734"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="58454734">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/58454734/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>While <code>recursive</code> is an experimental option of <code>fs.rmdir</code></p>

<pre><code>function rm (path, cb) {
    fs.stat(path, function (err, stats) {
        if (err)
            return cb(err);

        if (stats.isFile())
            return fs.unlink(path, cb);

        fs.rmdir(path, function (err) {
            if (!err || err &amp;&amp; err.code != 'ENOTEMPTY') 
                return cb(err);

            fs.readdir(path, function (err, files) {
                if (err)
                    return cb(err);

                let next = i =&gt; i == files.length ? 
                    rm(path, cb) : 
                    rm(path + '/' + files[i], err =&gt; err ? cb(err) : next(i + 1));

                next(0);
            });
        });
    });
}
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div id="answer-63099423" class="answer" data-answerid="63099423"  itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="63099423">
        <button class="js-vote-up-btn grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="This answer is useful" aria-pressed="false" aria-label="Up vote" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="m0 svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M2 26h32L18 10 2 26z"/></svg></button>

            <div class="js-accepted-answer-indicator grid--cell fc-green-500 ta-center py4 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Loading when this answer was accepted&#x2026;" tabindex="0" role="note" aria-label="Accepted">
                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"/></svg>
            </div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="/posts/63099423/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" title="Show activity on this post." aria-label="Timeline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"/></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<pre><code>const fs = require(&quot;fs&quot;);
fs.rmdir(&quot;./test&quot;, { recursive: true }, (err) =&gt; {
  if (err) {
    console.error(err);
  }
});

</code></pre>
<p>Provide the <code>recursive: true</code> option. And it will recursively delete all the files and directories of the given path. (Assuming <code>test</code> is directory present at root. )</p>
    </div>

    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="62874078">

    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<h1>🚀 <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/graph-fs" rel="nofollow noreferrer">graph-fs</a></h1>
<hr />
<p>Install</p>
<pre><code>npm i graph-fs
</code></pre>
<hr />
<p>Use</p>
<pre class="lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>const {Node} = require(&quot;graph-fs&quot;);
const directory = new Node(&quot;/path/to/directory&quot;);

directory.delete(); // &lt;--
</code></pre>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<pre class="lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>const fs = require("fs")
const path = require("path")

let _dirloc = '&lt;path_do_the_directory&gt;'

if (fs.existsSync(_dirloc)) {
  fs.readdir(path, (err, files) =&gt; {
    if (!err) {
      for (let file of files) {
        // Delete each file
        fs.unlinkSync(path.join(_dirloc, file))
      }
    }
  })
  // After the 'done' of each file delete,
  // Delete the directory itself.
  if (fs.unlinkSync(_dirloc)) {
    console.log('Directory has been deleted!')
  }
}
</code></pre>
    </div>
